**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? -> `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? -> `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? -> `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? -> `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? -> `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search -> read -> references -> definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Cross-Org WebIDL to DOM Binding Discovery

## Your Task

Find all WebIDL interface files in `mozilla-firefox/firefox` under `dom/webidl/` that define DOM interfaces for the Fetch API (Request, Response, Headers, FetchEvent). Then find the corresponding C++ binding implementation files under `dom/fetch/` that implement these WebIDL interfaces. Report the WebIDL file, the C++ header, and the C++ implementation file for each Fetch API type.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossorg domain.

## Available Resources

No local repositories are pre-checked out.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/firefox--871325b8` (mozilla-firefox/firefox)

## Fetch API WebIDL → C++ Binding Mapping

### Request
- **WebIDL**: `dom/webidl/Request.webidl` — defines `interface Request` (Exposed to Window and Worker) with constructor, method/url/headers/mode/credentials/cache/redirect/integrity/signal attributes, and `RequestInit` dictionary.
- **C++ Header**: `dom/fetch/Request.h` — `class Request final : public FetchBody<Request>, public nsWrapperCache`; uses `Request_Binding::Wrap`.
- **C++ Implementation**: `dom/fetch/Request.cpp`

### Response
- **WebIDL**: `dom/webidl/Response.webidl` — defines `interface Response` (Exposed to Window and Worker) with static methods (error, redirect, json), status/headers/body attributes, and `ResponseInit` dictionary.
- **C++ Header**: `dom/fetch/Response.h` — `class Response final : public FetchBody<Response>, public nsWrapperCache`; uses `Response_Binding::Wrap`.
- **C++ Implementation**: `dom/fetch/Response.cpp`

### Headers
- **WebIDL**: `dom/webidl/Headers.webidl` — defines `interface Headers` (Exposed to Window and Worker) with append/delete/get/has/set methods, `HeadersInit` typedef, and `HeadersGuardEnum`.
- **C++ Header**: `dom/fetch/Headers.h` — `class Headers final : public nsISupports, public nsWrapperCache`; backed by `InternalHeaders`.
- **C++ Implementation**: `dom/fetch/Headers.cpp`

### FetchEvent
- **WebIDL**: `dom/webidl/FetchEvent.webidl` — defines `interface FetchEvent : ExtendableEvent` (Exposed to ServiceWorker only, gated by `ServiceWorkersEnabled`), with request/preloadResponse/clientId/handled attributes and `respondWith()`.
- **C++ Header**: `dom/serviceworkers/ServiceWorkerEvents.h` — `class FetchEvent final : public ExtendableEvent`; includes `FetchEventBinding.h`.
